Adama TARAWORE - Kidali, min bɛ bɔ Mali juguya kɔnɔ, kɛra jamanaw cɛkow baara bolodalen ye kabini dɔgɔkun damadɔ.
Jamana minisiri caman ka taama kɔfɛ, a dakun sera Alize baarataabolo Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ka kulu de ma ka bila cɛmancɛlafanga mɔgɔw ka bolo kan kabini san 7 kɔnɔ.
An bɛ yɔrɔ jan na min na Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ Musa Mara tun bɛ a ka taama ka taa dugu kɔnɔ, san 2014.
Kabini o don, kow taara ni kulu marifatigiw ye, minnu bɛ Kidali ni jamana cɛmancɛ ɲɛmɔgɔya la ɲɛmɔgɔya la.
San kɔnɔ, ka ɲɛsin Mali kannabilala ɲɛmɔgɔw ma cogo min, o ɲɛbilala.
Cɛ sigilenw yɛrɛ yɛrɛ ka gɛlɛya k’u yɛrɛ makɔnɔ, wa, jamanaw cɛ kow ka kɔkɔrɔdonw b’a dɔn ko sankɛmɛ ɲɛmɔgɔw ye jihadikɛlaw ye, n’u foyi tɛ u ka jamana nin yɔrɔ cogoya ɲɔgɔn na.
San kɔnɔ, siyako ani hakililako clivage, min tun bɛ bila ɲɔgɔn na i n’a fɔ Igihadu ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, yɛlɛmana kosɛbɛ.
Gati ka tɛ dɔwɛrɛ la ka dugu tiɲɛ fanga fɛ, ka tɛmɛ El Haji Gamu fɛ a n’a y’u libre ka wuli ka yɔrɔ dala dugu kɔnɔ.
Jatigɛjatigɛwalew kɛra dɔgɔya, wa musow ani denmisɛnw musomaniw waleyaliw, minnu tiɲɛna ni kulu marifatigiw fɛ, quasima tununna.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, Kidali tora i n’a fɔ muso fatali, k’a to ale ka cɛsirikow an’a ka farikolo ɲɛtaaw b’a la.
O kɔfɛ, a y’a ɲɛsin a mɔgɔw la, ka tɛmɛ kumalasesɛbɛn dɔ fɛ, min bɛ sɔrɔdasi yɔrɔkelen fila sigili Gɔrma kɔnɔ, Azawadi tɔnw ka kolatilenjɛkulu (SEMA) fɛ.
A ma kɛ ni waleyali ye, deli ka kan ka kɛ kanu la, SEMA ka ɲɛmɔgɔw ka fɔ la, minnu b’a fɔ k’u bɛ waleya kɛ jama minnu ye magaliw kɔnɔ.
Nka SEMA ka wulikajɔ fɔɲɔgɔnya ma bɔ Malidenw dusumakasa, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la sigidajama dɔw.
Ka kɛɲɛ ni sigikafɔla mara kɔrɔnfɛla mɔgɔw ye, a tɛ sigi sen kan ko kulu, min labɛnnen don ani kɛlen tora Kidali, ka janfa kɛ gɔfɛrɛnaman ye gɔfɛrɛnaman kan, min bɛ lakanabaliya joli la.
Ka bɔ Iwɔgɔw ka toli la yaasa ka don yɔrɔw la ni sɔrɔdatuguli tɛ sɔrɔdasi bolo o ye sɔrɔdasi fɛɛrɛ ye min tɛ bɔ gɔfɛrɛnaman fɛ o min ka ɲɛfɔlɔ kɛra sababu ye k’a faamuya ko SEMA y’a kɛ a yɛrɛden ye nin gafe kɔnɔ.
A ɲɛ bɛɛ la, Ifoghas hakiliw y’u lafaamuya nin kalo laban ninnu kɔnɔ, n’a bɔra 2020 la, yɔrɔ min na, wo k’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ, faraɲɔgɔnkankulu Waaregew ye Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn ani bɛnɲini kama falenni kama sɔn.
Jamana kumaɲɔgɔnya kologɛlɛyali kan Bamako desanburukalo san 2019, Kidali cakɛda mɔgɔw y’u tiɲɛ dantigɛ k’u bɛɛ sɛmɛntiya Mali la wa fana n’a bɛ fɛn ye.
Nin kɔrɔfɔ kɛbagaw dɔ, Musa Agi Atahɛri, ye Denmisɛnw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri ye sisan.
Kidali dugulen mɔgɔ caman wɛrɛw bɛ gɔfɛrɛnaman kɔnɔ, i n’a fɔ Alhamudu Agi Iliyɛni, Malidenw minisiri min bɛ kɔkan, minnu sigilen don kɔkan.
Nin Iwɔgɔw ka togoda latigɛla ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ADUTE perezidan kɔrɔn tɛ mɔgɔ dɔ ye Kidali jamana tariku kɔnɔ.
Ni minisiriw ani jamana ɲɛmɔgɔw ka ciyakɛdaw seginna Kidali taama kɔnɔ, siga t’a la, k’a da o gɔfɛrɛnaman ka boloda bila denmisɛnw bolo, min tora jamana ka gɛlɛya ye.
Umaru KONATE - Halisa, diɲɛmɔgɔ tɔɲɔ bɛɛ ka taa ɲɛtaa vitesse la, Mali la.
A y’i cɛsiri k’a fɔ ko cɛmancɛlafanga tɛ.
Kabini san 1991 la, hali n’a yɛrɛ sɔrɔ nin jamana cɛmancɛ la, minnu y’a yɛrɛ dila k’u filsɛ ye.
Mɔgɔ b’o ko, an b’a yɛlɛma wa u tɛ fadenya la.
A ɲɛfɔlen bɛ ka ɲɛfɔ cogoya politiki cogoya la jamana kɔnɔ kabini san tan ni saba bɔ.
Ni politikimɔgɔw bɛ kulekule nin hohaho la, fasojama, a fɛ, bɛɛni, agoni ani végète misɛnnin na, kasɔrɔ farati tɛ min na.
Juguman na, a sumayara ka na.
Bamakɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, mɔgɔ minnu bɛ Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la, b’a miiri k’o ye cɛw yɛlɛmani ye, min bɛna ɲɛfɛ.
Olu ( Bamakɔw ) t’a dɔn ko kɛcogo de bɛ kofɔ wɛrɛ la, w’a tɛ cɛw de la.
O de kosɔn, u bɛ sira kan tuma bɛɛ, k’a ɲɛsin X walima Y walima Dɔgɔtɔrɔ walima Kɔgɔduguya ma, tuma min na, u tɛ fɔ a ka kow la, kasɔrɔ u y’i kan to k’a kɔfɛ.
O de kɛra san 2020 kɔnɔ ni diinɛmɔgɔ dɔw bɔli ye ɲɔgɔn na ani MISNKI – RFIPE sortiew.
U jiginafaamuyaba kɔrɔla Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la, k’u sen don loubardsɛmɛ caman kan dɔgɔkun caman kɔnɔ, ni ka perezidan, Ibarahima Bubakari Keyita, ka dɛmɛni ɲini, demokarasi na, o n’a ta bɛɛ.
U ka kɛlɛ kɔnɔ, u ma se ka hakili jigin Malidenw kan ka jamana ka hɛrɛ nataw la, IBeKa kɔfɛ, san 2020 utikalo tile 18 sanfɛ. Sɔrɔdasiya bolodalen min bɛ na ni sɔrɔdasiya bolodalen ye, o bɛ na ni burudamɛmɔgɔ dɔw ye minnu bɛ na komagɛlɛya ani frustrationi kɛ MIS – RFIPE jɔyɔrɔtigiw fɛ, minnu bɛ na bala ka bɔ u yɔrɔ la ni sɔrɔdasiya bolodalenw bɛɛ ye, minnu fɛra sɔrɔdasiya bolodiɲɛbila kokura
U ka fɔ la, fanga tun b’u yɛrɛ sɔrɔ.
Tiɲɛ na, ɲagali tɛ ba la Mali kɔnɔ, nka a bɛ mandiya n’a yɛrɛ ɲɛ.
Demokarati dɔw, minnu bɛ fɛ ka fanga taa bɔlɔlɔ kan.
A ma kɛnɛ kan, sɔrɔdasi denmisɛnw ma se k’u ka jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw ta ka ɲɛsin fasojama ma min sonyalen b’a la ka hɛrɛ kama.
I n’a fɔ cogo min na, jalakiw bɛ kɛ kunbalan ye, fasojama jigi b’a kan an’a bɛ jigiya ni ladiyali ye.
Kuru sarati!
Gɔfɛrɛnaman dɔ sigili sen kan ka kɛ forcepikaw ye, kow tɛ ka daminɛ ka bila.
Cɛmancɛlafanga kolatigɛjɛkulu ( SEYNITE ) bɛ bila sen kan a kɛcogoya kelenw kɔnɔ, janko k’a sababu kɛ Mali jɛrɛjɛkulu jɛrɛkulu fitini ye, o min belebele bɛ bɛnkansɛbɛn ani ɲɔgɔnfaamuya, minnu y’a laɲini olu fɛ, ci n’a fɔ la.
Bingoya ani danayako bɛna kɛ Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la.
Cɛmancɛlafanga bolofara ani sɔrɔdasi minnu bɛ fanga kɔnɔ tɛ kelen ɲɛ fɛ.
Kɔlɔsili ye mɛkalo tile 24 san 2021 fangabin ye.
Tariku taamasiyɛnna na,
Cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan, Mahan Nda, an’a ka minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Mukutari Wani, bilala ntolatan na, mara cɛmancɛlafanga laban kɔnɔntɔn kɔnɔntɔn, o kɛra fasojama jigiya kan.
Yɛlɛmaw tagara i n’a fɔ gɛlɛya bannen don walasa ka jigi waro.
Sɔrɔdasiw ka fanga ɲɛmɔgɔ y’a ŋaniya ka kow ta bolo la.
O kɛli kama, fɛnsɔrɔw bɛ caya ni Mali jɛrɛjɛkulu mɔgɔw bɛɛ ye.
O daminɛni kama, partɛn ɲuman bɛ kɛ musɛnki rɛfupe la, min b’a ka ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu perezidan sigi, walasa k’a kɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔ la.
Nin taabolo ye tɔn in kokɛbagaw bolo, minnu bɛ wuli ka sebaaya sɔrɔ, n’a ye ɲininkaliw ye, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, bawo filɛlikɛla caman sen b’a la.
A bɛ sɔrɔdasi fɛn min ye sɔridasi dɔ ye, Sogɛli Mayiga bɛ na kɛ mɔgɔ dɔw ye profil-baso kɛ yaasa ka yɛrɛlakɔrɔfɛnw lafasa walima k’a kɔn politiki hakilila lafasa?Chogɛli Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, o ye kɛlɛ belebele ye wolodenya murutili Tɔnba ye.
PEYRI.
Kabini san 1991, o pariti b’a ɲini ka sira sɔrɔ politiki sira kan.
Sogɛli sɔnɔ ka kɛ Minisiri ɲɛmɔgɔ ye, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita y’a ɲini k’a ko sɔridasi walew politikikɛnɛ kan politikimɔgɔw caman bɛ minnu na, o minnu, Sogɛli bɛ minnu kɔnɔ kabini san bisaba?
Kasɔrɔ a ma kɛnɛ kan, gɔfɛrɛnaman nata bɛ na kɛ fanba mɔgɔw ye, minnu bɛ musɛnki ɲɛmɔgɔw bolo.
Sogɛli la, anw b’a fɔ ko pariti dɔ ncinin dɔ walima kulu ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu fan dɔ ɲɛnabɔcogoya bɛ Jamana kɔnɔn bawo ko dafɛnw an’a ɲanakow tɛ danfaraw ye.
Minnu b’a la k’a fɔ ko Sogɛli ye kow cogoya cɛ in cɛ in kanu na, u ka kan ka joli sɔrɔ.
Cɛ min jalatigɛ ka tɛmɛ baara kan an’a kɔrɔfɔ tɛ.
MI SNKI RFIPE fɛɛrɛ jɛkuluɲɛmɔgɔ y’a kɛ fanga kura ye, mɔgɔ b’a faamuya k’a fɔ ko nin tɛ kɛ ka Mali kan, nk’a ka sugolako lataa kɛ tiɲɛ na.
Sogɛli bɛna bila ɲɛ o ɲɛ fɛ a tun bɛ fɛ ka kɛlɛ durɔn musɛnki rɛfupe sortiew la wa cɛ gɛlɛyaba don cɛ ka fɛn fuu ye.
Kɔkɔrɔdon caman, minnu bɛ fɔ fanga ɲɛ yɔrɔ ma, tɛ fɛ ka baara ɲɛ bila cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔw kura ma, bawo, an bɛ mɔgɔ kɔkɔrɔdon ni waleyaw ye, ani tɛmɛ tɛ kumakanw kan, kɛnɛ kan walima taamasiyɛnw.
Malidenw bɛɛ tɛ mago sɔrɔ tile saba.
baarakɛden ka pani bɛ dabila dɔgɔkun kɔnɔ.
kiriyɔrɔw bɔlen do gɛlɛyalakaw bolo.
mɔgɔ joginnenw bɛɛ dafɛ,
Jamana bɛɛlajɛlen bɛ kulu marifatigiw ka maramafɛnw kɔnɔ wa, ɲankata bɛ Bamako.
Malidenw tɛ yaala kelen pe de ye.
Waati sera tɛmɛna kofɔlenw ma walima politiki ŋaniyaw bagabagaw ma.
I n’a fɔ cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan kura y’a fɔ cogo min, fɔlɔ kelen pe min na, o ye waati ye.
O la, walasa k’a ɲɛfɔ Maliden 20 ɲɔgɔn kan ko, a bɛ se ka ka Mali kura sɔrɔ, Sogɛli ka kan ka boulevardi minnu ɲɔgɔn ma sariyasɔsɔbagaw fɛ, ka dɔ bɔ fasoden gansanw kan an ka siraw kɔnɔ, ka tugu ntolanw lakanani ani laban na, ɲankata kɛlɛli, yɛrɛmayɔrɔbaliya, nɔfɛtaama ani nafolo ɲankata kɔnɔ.
Politiki walima ɲuman waliyali, a bɛ lahidu ta Malidenw ye.
Jɔnni ka kan ka bɔ ni mɔgɔ ɲɔgɔn ye walima mun ye ɲɔgɔn ye?
Ni rupture ani misali ye, a ka kan ka kɛ, Sogɛli b’a dɔn k’a fɔ mɔgɔ min b’a la k’o tɛ ale de ka kan ka kɛ baara ye.
A bɛ don mɔgɔ minnu ni minnu cɛ ka kan ka jɔ wa a ka misali tɛ mɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ n’a y’a sɔrɔ a kalekanw kɔrɔ.
Cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛbilala Kabini, cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛbilala Jamana kunna quantɛ cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛminɛ ma.
Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, a ka saratiwaati kɔnɔ, y’a jira k’a fɔ k’a bɛna kɛ Jamana Kumaɲɔgɔnya bɛɛ sen bɛ min na komagɛlɛyaliw kan cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔya kama kalo kɔnɔ minnu tɛmɛnenw la.
Fan wɛrɛ fɛ, a ka Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ bɛ jamana assisesɛbɛn kura labɛnni ɲɛmɔgɔya yani fanga bɛɛ kama walasa ka cɛmancɛlafanga ta ɲɛtaa.
Ka taa yɔrɔ min na, Sogɛli bɛ taa yɔrɔ jan na min t’a yɛrɛ kofɔ.
Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kura ka waleyaw bɛ sɔsɔli kɛ nin ɲɛfɔli ye.
K’a kɔdon ko yɛrɛ ma, min ye fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw labɛnni ye, walasa ka laban kalataw labɛnni na, u ka kan ka kɛ sariyasɔsɔliw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛlabɛnni ye, waati caman tɛ ka taama kunw la, minnu ma kɛ sababu ye ka latigɛ ɲuman ta.
Nin taamaw ani kumaɲɔgɔnyaw, anw ye joli min kɛ kaban nin jamana kɔnɔ.
Min ye farali koɲɛ ɲɔgɔn kan, Sogɛli dun bɛ ko wulikajɔ kɔnɔ ni cɛmancɛlafanga bɛnkansariya ye, ni a ka fangaɲɔgɔnma mɔgɔba ( 28 ) ye.
Min ye tilali ye mɔgɔw bɛɛ ladon fleew kɔnɔ, n’a yɔrɔ ka don, o yɔrɔ ka don kosɛbɛ.
Gɔfɛrɛnaman kura sigilen bɛ mɔgɔw, minnu sirilen don M5, sɔrɔdasiw, kulu marifatigiw ani mɔgɔba dɔw, minnu diyanyeko dɔrɔmɛlen don diinɛ ɲɛmɔgɔ dɔw fɛ.
Politiki ani jɛrɛjɛkuluw fanba, jɔda bɛ min kɔnɔ, bɛ nin ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ cogo la.
O ko in tɛ fɛ ka jamana sigida assisesɛbɛnw kɛli minnu bɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ ka dusu don ɲɛ.
Kow wɛrɛw, minnu bɛ ɲininkaliw chez jamana ka nata la, nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɔnɔ, min taamasiyɛnna kaban kaban, ni yâtonnement ye kaban.
Donan.
Lebedem.
Mɔgɔ kana kɛ mɔgɔ ka faamu ko Alize baarataabolo Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛna kɛ fan dɔ fɛ wa a fan wɛrɛw la.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala fan bɛɛ mɔgɔw bɛ fɛn minnu bɛ fɛ ka don Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
Fo ka bɔ Bɛnkansɛbɛn kalanni kura ma.
Nin ye nɔnikɛyɔrɔ ye, min ka kan ka kɛ kojugu.
ye SEMA mɔgɔ minnu tun bɛ Bamakɔ, kunnafonidi lajɛba dɔ senfɛ, Kunnafonidilaw ka soba la, karidon tɛmɛnen.
U tun ye Ataye Agi Mohamɛdi ye cidenkulu ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, Med Almayulud Uludi Ramadani, kumalasela, Sidi Agi Baye ani Tila Agi Zeyini bɛ minnu cɛla, minnu tun bɛ SEMA ka cidenkuluw bɛɛ ye Bamakɔ, Bɛnkansɛbɛn waliyali ɲɛkɔrɔ kunnafonidilaw ɲɛkɔrɔ, san 6 bɛnkansɛbɛn min bɔra Alize taabolo la bɛnkansɛbɛn na.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɔli koɲɛ kan, min bɛ tali kɛ Alize baarataabolo Bɛnkansɛbɛn na, SEMA mɔgɔw, minnu tun bɛ lajɛ, bɛɛ bɛn’a ma ko nin sababu ye kokɛyɔrɔ belebele ye, min tɛ ka kan ka dabila.
U ka kumalasela, Alɔmudulu Ulidi Ramadani, ka fɔ la, bolonɔbilali fan bɛɛ mɔgɔw bɛ jɛn ni bɛnkanw ye, u bɛ fɛ k’u don minnu na.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɔlen bɛ na kɛ sababu ye an ka fɛn o fɛn lasɔrɔ, an ka fɛn o fɛn ma se ka bɔ Alize.
a y’o dantigɛ.
Fan si ma fɔ Bɛnkansɛbɛn sɔrɔ.
Anw ye diɲɛmɔgɔw yɛrɛ minnu y’a to an ka bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɛbila.
An tun tɛ fɔ kɛnɛ kan.
Tilla Agi Zeyini y’o da tulow kan.
Jɛkulu cilenw bolo, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛ lajɛlen don fanba kɔnɔ, minnu ye Jamana ka sagotigiya ye, jamana kelenyatɔn, jamana dugukolo sigili ani jamana perezidansigikalata ye.
Ni fan kelen-kelen b’a hakilijakabɔ k’a fɔ ko nin domainew lakodɔnnen don, fan dɔ bɛ se ka jɛkulu min bɛ Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔ (SEYSIYA) lamini kama.
Adara y’o ɲɛfɔ, walasa k’a ɲɛfɔli kɛ, minnu bɛna se ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn waleya ka bila sen kan.
O yɔrɔ ninnu tɛ, yɛlɛma wɛrɛ si tɛ.
O labɛnni kura bɛ se ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn bila bɛnkan wɛrɛw la minnu tɛ na kuncɛ.
O bɛna kɛ lafiya Bɛnkansɛbɛn waliyali bali.
lajɛ kumakɛlaw y’a ɲɛfɔ yani k’u hakililatigɛ ko nin lawaliyali tɛna kɛlɛ koli ye kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Mali ni kulu marifatigiw cɛ.
Politiki kan, gɛlɛya bɛɛ politiki la, min bɛ tali kɛ ani min ma lakodɔn, o kɔfɛ kɛra gɛlɛya seginni ye.
Hakilila don bɛɛ la.
O kandi tɛ jɔ, mɔgɔ tɛ se ka tiɲɛtigiya k’a fɔ ko gɛlɛya tɛna kɛ.
Ataye Agi Mohamɛdi ye jalatigi ɲɛmɔgɔ ye.
K’a kɔdon o la SEMA hakilila bɛ to yen, ka tɛmɛ cɛmancɛlafanga fɛ.
Cɛmancɛlafanga gɔfɛrɛnaman, ka tɛmɛ Cɛmancɛlafanga Perezidan fɛ, ma baloko dɔ jira an ɲɛsin Bɛnkansɛbɛn waleyali ma.
A nana fɛn dɔ ka bɔ an bolo, min b’a jira k’a fɔ ko a ŋaniya t’a bolo.
A. Ataye y’a da kɛnɛ kan, a kɛtɔla k’a ka kuma falenniw latigɛ Cɛmancɛlafanga Perezidan, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, ka fɔ la, Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn waliyali ɲuman ye.
SEMA b’a yɛrɛ dantigɛ k’a bɛ na segin ka bɛnkansɛbɛn kan, fo ka taa SEYNITE (CNT) la.
SEMA ka nalen bɛ k’a ka kunnafonidi lajɛrɛ dɔ labɛn Bamakɔ, ni k’u ka hakililatigɛ bila yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya ani lakana kan.
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko kiri bɔra a la ani k’u kanda daminɛna a kɛ.
Jɛkulu ɲɛmɔgɔba, Atayi Agi Mohamɛdi, y’o jɔ dantigɛ.
Kureyisi Sise.
BɛnkanSɛbɛn NA Bɛnkansɛbɛn waliyali San wɔɔrɔ kɔfɛ, a lawaliyali gɛlɛyaw bɛ min kɔnɔ. Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala san 2015 mɛkalo tile 15, o kɔfɛ zuwɛnkalo tile 20, bɛn ani bɛnɲini kama Mali la. Bɛnkansɛbɛn, min bɛ bɔ Alize taabolo la, san wɔɔrɔ ɲɔgɔnna kɔ, a lawaliyali gɛlɛyaw bɛ kɔnɔ.
Mali kɛlɛbolo ka jigin kɔnɔ Kidali, bin banba la wa min y’i yɛrɛ faga.
O la, ɲɛmɔgɔw ye kumaɲɔgɔnyaw kɛ Alizeri kɔnɔ ni (SEMA) rebelli kɔrɔw ye diɲɛmɔgɔw ka dɔgɔya kɔnɔ waati kɔnɔntɔn de kɔnɔ minnu y’a to mɔgɔ fila ka ɲɔgɔnfaamuya kɛnɛ kan.
Mali ɲɛmɔgɔw ka laɲini kɔfɛ, bolonɔbilali Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala Bamakɔ, mɛkalo tile 15 san 2015 ani zuwɛnkalo tile 20 san o kɔnɔ, mɔgɔ minnu tun tɛ bannenw ye.
San wɔɔrɔ kɔfɛ, bolonɔbilala bɛnkansɛbɛn min bɔra Alize baarataabolo la, bɛ to ka wulikajɔ ni wulikajɔ caman di mɔgɔw fɛ, minnu y’u ka bolonɔbilala kɛ.
Wa, n’an ka kan ka san wɔɔrɔ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw bakurubajate jateminɛ, min ye kulu marifatigiw bolonɔbilali kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ani Mali kɛlɛbolo, a waleyali tolen don halibi SEYSIYAW danfaralenw cɛ, wa, n’an y’an ka sɛgɛsɛgɛliw kɔrɔ, nin kunfɛsigiw bɛ kɛ a baarakɛbagaw (kulu marifatigi ani Jamana ) fɛ, minnu bɛ lanɔgɔya kɛ dɔwɛrɛ la tuma dɔw, fan dɔ fɛ ani fan wɛrɛ fɛ, n’o ye gafe in labɛnni ye jama fɛ.
O de y’a to mɔgɔ sigilenw ka tɛmɛ bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
Munna, min na, bi, bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛ bolonkɔnɔbila, yɛlɛmaba si ma se ka bila sen kan, kasɔrɔ tilalidenw, minnu ma bɔ kɛlɛ walew la, y’u sigi, u ka marifabila kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen don ani ka Mali kɔgɔduguyanfan sɔrɔdasiw domini la, wa u bɛ ka bolonkɔnɔn bila jama kuluw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, minnu bɛ kɛ Sahɛli la.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, nizɛri jamana kuntigi kɔrɔ, Mahamadu Isufu, y’a fɔ ko siga tɛ min na, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali sen kan bɛ marabolo kɔnɔn ani ko.
Kidali ye bagabaga ye Nizɛri kɔnɔna lakana la.
Sidi Brahimu Ulidi Sidati tɔden, min ye Alizeri bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɛbila, min ye bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɛbila, Azawadi tɔnw ka Koladilanjɛkulu (SEMA) ye dumuni ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bila boloɲɔgɔnw bolonɛbila kɔnɔ, minnu cɛsirilen bɛ bɛn ani ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ Mali kɔnɔ.
Ni Abudulayi Umaru Jɔpu ka nali ye Kɔkankow ani Jamanaw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ bolodiɲɔgɔnma cakɛdaba la, ani min ye nin bɛnkansɛbɛn nin bolonɛbila ye, an jigi b’a kan ko a bɛna dadigi kɛ a waleyali la.
Usamani Mahamani - Kɛlɛbolofara fɔlɔw labaarali, sɔrɔdasi ka bolofara fɔlɔw labaarali, DEDEYRI, yiriwali baarabolodaliw, minnu fɔra, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla, nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɔnɔ, min tɛna kɛ. Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn ani bɛnɲini min bɔra Alize taabolo la, ani diɲɛmɔgɔw ye, olu sɔrɔ, kun ye, ka ɲɔgɔnye kɛ Kidali.
Fɔlɔ fɔlɔ kabini bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala san 2015 cɛmaɲiw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A ɲinini fɔlɔ tun kɛra sɛtanburukalo la sɛtanburukalo la.
Ani fana fanga gɔfɛrɛnaman fɛ, ani fana mɔgɔ kuluw maramafɛntigiw ani diɲɛmɔgɔw fɛ, taama ka taa Kidali, mɔgɔ caman tun ka ɲɛ o la, ka nin taamasiyɛn daga kura taamasiyɛnna hukumu kɔnɔ.
Gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔ Six ye taama kɛ.
Kolonɛli - mazɔri Isimayeli Wage ( Jamana bɛnɲini ), Mamadu Mohamɛdi Kulibali ( Jamana Labɛn kura ), Mohamɛdi Saliya Ture ( Baara ni Baaradilabaara kalan ), Kolonɛli Modibo Kone ( Lakana ani Sigida la ), Bintu Funɛ Samake ( Musow ka baara ani Den banni ) ani Mahmudu Ulidi Mohamedi ( Agriculture, Jago ani Mɛnɛko ).
.
A faseri sɛbɛn kan « Irisu » la. San 2021 kalosaba fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola daman ye sanu ɔnsi 125.088 bɔ, k’a bɛn 7% ( ɔnsi 88.6 8 8 ) kan. BEDEGƆLɔdi Mali dugujukɔrɔfɛnw jɔyɔrɔtigiw ye ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 14 tɛmɛnen, u daga kɔnɔ, n’a bɛ damana ye Nizɛri Cɛmancɛlafanga la, u ka san kunnafonidilajɛ ɲɔgɔnyeba, sabanan 3nan.
Sababu, jɔyɔrɔtigiw ka jɛkabaara bakurubajate bɔ, gɛlɛyaw an’a nataw la.
U ye kunnafonidilaw ka setigiya gɛlɛya kan, min sirilen don Minankoto yɔrɔ fɛnbɔli yamaruyasɛbɛn dili kura na, Kenieba fɛ.
Lajɛba tun bɛ ka kɛ ni BedegɔlidiBuli Litili ɛmɔgɔba ye, a masurunna a masurunnabaaraɲɔgɔn caman fɛ.
A ka baara la, ɛmɔgɔba y’a dantigɛ ko san 2020 kɔnɔ, BedeGɔlidi – Mali cakɛda ye dɛmɛ kɛ Mali sɔrɔ ye, sefawari miliyari 34 na, saraw ani hadamadenya nafamafɛnw na baarakɛlaw ye.
San 2016 – 2020 waati kɔnɔ, Bull Litili, a ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw jɛkulu ye Sefa wari miliyari 162 ma Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye.
Kaɲaka sigida mɔgɔw ka yiriwalinafolobɔw sigibagaw ka fɔ la, DEZE ka fɔ la, bɛ minnu na Sefa wari miliyari 2,1 ye, ani Sefa wari miliyari 82 ye, minnu tara fɛnw tali la Mali la.
Fekola daminɛ, sɔrɔ ani nataw. BedeGɔlidi – Mali jɔyɔrɔtigiba y’a da tulow kan ko san 2020 kɔnɔ Fekola daminɛ b’a ka sanu ɔnsi miliyari 622.000 bɔ, k’a jate tɔni 18 ye.
San 2021 kalosaba fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola daman ye sanu ɔnsi 125.088 bɔ, k’a bɛn 7% ( ɔnsi 88.6 8 ) ma, ka tɛmɛ a ɲɛsigilen kan, a y’o ɲɛfɔ, yani a y’a jira k’a fɔ ko san 2021 kɔnɔ, Fekola daman tun ka kan ka sanu ɔnsi 530.000 ni 560.000 cɛ ( ɔnsi 16 ɲɔgɔnna ), bɔli musakaw la, minnu bɛ IYSI dolari 405 ni 445 cɛ ( IYSI dolari 245.000 cɛ ).
Min bɛ musaka la ( PEYRIZE ), bɛ bɔ IYSI dolari 745 ni 785 cɛ ( ka bɔ Sefa wari miliyari 432.000 la ).
Sigida la San 2020 laban na, BedeGɔlidi tun bɛ Maliden 2.053 ani jamana wɛrɛ 130 la.
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko an ka baarakɛdenjɔn 90 % bɛ ye Mali ye, a y’o dantigɛ, ani k’a fara a kan ko An b’a to sigida baarasigiw ka kan caya, n’an bɛ ɲini ka baara ɲiniw fara ɲɔgɔn kan sigida ani jamana la.
Hadamadenyako ani sigidajama yiriwali siratigɛ la. O siratigɛ fɛ, lajɛ kumakɛla y’a da kɛnɛ kan ko 2021 baarabolodali kuraw jirala ani k’u latigɛ ka kɛ Keɲeba yiriwali Waleyali ɛmɔgɔyakulu fɛ.
Nin ɲɔgɔnna kɔnɔ, baarabolodali tan ni fila ye, minnu jirala ani k’u lakodɔn, Hakili ɲɛmɔgɔya la, Fadugu, Medinandi, Tintiba, Maleya, Bilaliba, Kolomba ani Sokɔndi, k’a fara Fekola ani Betekili kan.
Bulɛlitili ka fɔ la, a ka baarabolodaliw musaka jate sigira sefawari miliyon 300 ma.
Fekola ka tilebinyanfan kɔnɔ. Bili Litili ka fɔ la, a ka usine Fekola, o ye tilebinyanfan filanan ye, min bɛ BEDEGƆlidi kɔnɔn.
Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye Fekola S.A. dugujukɔrɔfɛn jɛkulu « dɔgɔtɔrɔ » 80%, min bɛ ka baara kɛ Keɲeba sɛrikili la, bɛ BedeGɔlidi kɔnɔ ani 20% bɛ Mali Jamana fɛ.
kunnafonidilaw ɲininkaliw y’a fanba kɛ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, Minankoto fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn dili kɔfɛ, k’a sababu kɛ BedeGɔlidi ka miliyɔn 500 ɲɔgɔnna ye, i ko dɔ fara.
A ka jaabi kɔnɔ, Bili Litili DEZE y’o jalakili jira k’a fɔ ko banabaliw do.
A ka kumafɔw kɔfɛ k’a kɔdon a fɔlenw na, bakurubajate bɛ min kɔnɔ kunnafonidilaw B2Gɔlidi Mali ma wari sɔrɔ k’a sababu kɛ Minankoto yamaruyasɛbɛnbɔli kɛli ye.
A. M Ture - K’a kɔdon kunnafoni dɔw na, minisiri ɲɛmɔgɔyasɛbɛn, min bɛ tali kɛ mɛkalo tile 7 san 2021, n’o bɛ tali kɛ peyazi ani routigiyɔrɔw sigili kofɔ ani n’a bɛ mara saratiw tali kofɔ, bɛ ko goni kɛ.
Wa bisigikumaw, minnu bɛ sɛbɛnw sɔrɔli kofɔ, tɛ dɛsɛ dɔn de ye.
Fɔlɔ don ka minisirisariya min bɛ tali kɛ, ka fɔ k’a gɛlɛya min posé, walasa ka a ɲɛfɔli kɛ a la.
O minisirisariya minisirisariya, a sariyasen 2nan kɔnɔ, b’a dantigɛ ko mɔgɔ sigilenw bɛ bila ciyakɛyɔrɔ la, ni damatɛmɛ sɔsɔli ye, sariyaw labatoli kɔnɔ.
Sariyasen 3 b’a fɔ ko peyazi jɔyɔrɔ kelen, min bɛ tali kɛ bolimafɛn dɔ ye, bɛ bisigi kɛ ka peyazi warisaraw sarali ye, minnu sannayɛlɛtariw sigilen don nin cogo la.
Bagisɛbɛnw bolo, a dɔgɔyalen bɛ 150 la, ɲɔgɔndan ani tɛmɛtɔla.
Kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya bolimafɛnw (250, ɛsiyirɛ ani tɛmɛtɔla ).
Takisiw (Sefa wari 400, ɲɔgɔndan ani tɛmɛtɔla).
forobaminɛnw ci ka tɛmɛ mɔgɔ 25 personnesɛni kan (Sefa wari 300, ani tɛmɛ passage 150).
sojɔminɛnw donniw (Sefa wari 300, ɲɔgɔndan ani ci ta ).
Taamaw ani taamarakotakɛtaw, minnu ka ca ni mɔgɔ 25 ye ( Sefa wari 300 ani tɛmɛni kɛra ).
Baganmafɛnw ani mankanbagaw (Sefa wari 300, ɲɔgɔndan ani tɛmɛtɔla ).
Jɔda b’a la fana ka hakilijigin kɛ ko dugukolo hakɛ kan bɛ seginna san kelen kɔ, sentanya ka ɲɛsin bolimafɛnw magoɲɛsɔrɔ ma, k’a da bɛɛjɛwari kiimɛnan kan.
Wa peyazi ciyakɛyɔrɔ sigibagaw bɛ bisimilali yamaruyasɛbɛn dɔ kɛrɛntiya, min ciyakɛdaw ka kɛcogoya an’a wari hakɛ latigɛlen bɛ minisiri ka latigɛli la.
Fan wɛrɛ wɛrɛ fɛ, nin minisirisariya baarabolodali sariyasen 4 b’a fɔ ko peyazi ni pesagi cakɛda, min ma di mobili garabaga ma, bolo don a ɲɛmɔgɔ fɛ, fo ka bolibaga dɔ ciya.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn min bɔra a waleyali ni nin minisirisariya sariyasɛbɛn 2 waleyali fɛ, wari hakɛw bɛ na diɲɛ kɛnɛ kan, minnu ɲɛsigilen don a bɛnkansɛbɛn caman ka caya la.
Ani fana, ka fɔ la a ka sariyasen 7 la, koɲɛ ɲɛmɔgɔw minnu ka kan ni nin laadalatɔnsigi ye, olu ye.
Sirataw ɲɛmɔgɔba, Sigidaw ani dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔba, Sirakanna ɲɛmɔgɔba, Polisi ɲɛmɔgɔba, Lakana ɲɛmɔgɔba, Sigidalamɔgɔw ka ɲɛmɔgɔba, Jamana sariyasunba ɲɛmɔgɔba,
Fɛn bɛɛ bɛ kɛ!
Min ye a waleyali kɛnɛ kan, a bɛ kɛ koɲuman n’a ye foli kɛcogo ye, a kɛra min kan a kɔlɔsili ɲɛmɔgɔba fɛ, Lala Koyɛte, ka tɔgɔlasigi dɔ senfɛ.
hadamadenyaɲɔgɔnw ka jɛɲɔgɔn kan.
O sababu la, routiɲɛmɔgɔ ɲɛmɔgɔba, Lala Koyɛti, y’a ɲini ka jɔrɔtigiya bila sɛbɛnw kologɛlɛyali la ani sɛbɛnw taabolow la.
A ka fɔ la, sɛbɛnw informatisénnen bɛ dannaw bɛɛ sɔrɔ, minnu ka kan.
Min ye sifilɛlisira sɛbɛnw ye, u bɛ labaara kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ani waatilabaara kɛ mɔgɔ kuraw la walima minnu bilala ka se k’u ka laɲiniw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la.
Sɛbɛn ninnu bɛ tali kɛ peyazi yɔrɔ, a yɔrɔ layɛrɛ, a farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔyaso ka yɔrɔ la, walasa k’a ka tiɲɛni ye.
Mmu Lala Koyɛti b’a hakilijigin kɛ k’a fɔ ko sɛbɛnw falsira sɛbɛn, k’a kɔdon kunnafoniw tɛ minnu bɛ fɛ, wa ko sɛbɛnw bɛna don nɛgɛsira kan, kabini sɛbɛnw bilala sen kan.
O tuma, fɛn bɛɛ bɛ ka kɛ mɔgɔ ɲuman ye waati la!
Burama Keyita - A bɛ kɛ bolonɔbila, min bɛ na kɛ, bɔlɔlɔ donni cakɛda yɛlɛma, san nata la, Bamakɔ dugu kiimɛnan kan.
O cakɛda, min bɛ na sigi Sankoroba komini kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Sinina, bɛna a don Bamakɔ jɔyɔrɔ la sigidajama hukumu kɔnɔ.
Bamakɔ Disiriki mɛri, Adama Sangare ani SIYAYRI Kɔnɔmɔgɔ, Jaje n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Amadu Sankare, Dugujukɔrɔfɛnkow, Kuranko ani Jiko minisiri, Lamini Sedu Tarawore, ye bolonɔbila laselisɛbɛn, min bɛ tali kɛ zuwɛnkalo tile 17 tɛmɛnen, Radisson Kolombiya la, bɛnkansɛbɛn dilan, min bɛ tali kɛ donkomini yɔrɔ la ani yɔrɔ donnibaara yɛrɛyɛrɛ cakɛda dilan ye.
Mɔgɔba caman tun bɛ min kɔnɔ, EYSIDEYSI Elekɛnɛmisɛn Yɛlɛri ɛmɔgɔ, SEYRI Kɔnɔmɔgɔw ka cakɛda, baarabolodali initia, Foye Ibarahima Mayiga, Sankara mɛri, tun bɛ min kɔnɔ.
Nin bɛnkansɛbɛn kura, min bolonɔbilala Disiriki Mayɛri ani SEYRI kulu fɛ, kun ye “Dɔbɔli de bɛɛjɛn”, min kɛra Bamakɔ dugu kɛnɛkɛnɛmabaarada yamaruya kɛ yen.
Nin baarabolodali, min b’a ɲini ka nɔgɔyada nɔgɔya, bɛ tiɲɛ na, siga t’a la, ka ɲɛsin ɲɛmɔgɔw ka ŋaniya juguya ma, ka nɔgɔyada nɔgɔya, jama ka hɛrɛ kama.
O de kosɔn, SEYVIZI mɛri, Adama Berethé, y’a ɲini cakɛda, min ka baara bolodalen bɛ u ka jɔyɔrɔtigiw bolo, fɛsɛfɛsɛ ka foyi si kɛ walasa a laɲini minnu ɲininen tɛ, ka tɛmɛ nin bɛnkansɛbɛn fɛ, ka ɲɛw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A baarabolodali ɲɛfɔli kɔnɔ, EYSIDE ɛmɔgɔba, Foye Ibarahima Mayiga, y’a dantigɛ k’a fɔ ko baarabolodali ka laɲini ye ka dɛmɛ don Bamakɔ Disiriki orduriyɛlɛri gɛlɛya la ani k’a fɔ ko dɛmɛ don baarakɛminɛnw ye nafa dɔ ye, a ka dɛmɛ kɛ minnu na Mali dunan kɔnɔn.
O faralankulu, min bɛ na sigi Sankoroba komini kɔnɔ, n’o ye Sinsina ye, bɛna kɛ Bamakɔ jɔyɔrɔ la sigidajama hukumu kɔnɔ.
Ale ka fɔ la, nin cakɛda bɛ na tɛmɛ 1200 bɔ, k’a ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɛ MW 40 ye.
A baara sefawari jate bɛ kɛ sefawari miliyari 130 na, a bɛna wolo dayɛlɛwaari 6000 la.
SEYRI Kɔnɔn ɲɛmɔgɔba, Jaje, n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Amadu Sankare, y’a pereperelatigɛ ko Sankara bolofara choixra walasa ka o cakɛda sigi, o tun tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye.
Ale ka fɔ la, a ka suruncakɔyɔrɔ ni tali daminɛni Guine-Sikasso-Bamako ni Bukulaɲɛgɛnkɛrɛyɔ fɛ.
Jira min kiimɛnan bɛ EDEYMU ma, bɛna minɛnw lasɔrɔ.
Yanni a k’a dantigɛ k’a fɔ ko lamini lakana ye fɛn ye, nin baarabolodali bɛ senna, ka tɛmɛ dɔwɛrɛ fɛ ani baarakɛcogo min bɛ kɛ nin finan kama.
A y’a lasɔrɔ ka wele bila bɛɛ lajɛlen na walasa ka baarabolodali ɲɛni a kama jamana ka nafa kama.
Nin cakɛda baaraw dili bɛ na dɛmɛ kɛ Bamakɔ dugu lasaniyali la.
Kuma wɛrɛ la, ka Bamakɔ dugu sigi. Ka kɛ Disiriki mɛri, Adama Sangare, la, siratigɛ la, ko labɛnnenw tɛ falen, nka Jamana ka ŋɛnɛya an’a bilasirali de bɛ min bolo tuma bɛɛ.
Yaan’a k’i nisɔndiyalen bɛ nin jɛɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bolonɛbila la a meri ani E2SIDE fɛ, ka dumafɛɛrɛw donni cakɛda yɛlɛma ka kɛ kɛnɛkanko ye.
A kɛtɔla ka kuma laban, a y’a ɲini bɛɛ ka bilasirali la a baarabolodali kama.
A. M Ture - Nin y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye, ko SEYSIYA ka ɲɔgɔnye bɛ kɛ Kidali, sɛbɛn caman kɔfɛ.
A kɛra Alizeri kɔkankow minisiri, SE Bɛnkankow minisiri, Sabiri Bukadumu, bolo, gɔfɛrɛnaman tɔgɔlamɔgɔ, Kolonɛli Isimayeli Wage ani Gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔ wɛrɛw, Pilatifɔrɔmu ni SEMA kuluw maramafɛntigiw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw, bɛ minnu na.
Minisima tɔgɔlamɔgɔ, min ye ɲɔgɔnye la, ye ɲɔgɔnye nɔgɔya ani kokɛda belebele ye, hali ni Mali fan wɛrɛ fɛ, ani diɲɛmɔgɔw ka kuma fɔ a ye.
S.E.M. Zan-Ywi Le Daniyan, Faransi jamana kɔkankow minisiri ani Afiriki polisikomisɛri, Sɛbɛn ani Afiriki polisiɲɛmɔgɔ, Sɛbɛn ani Afiriki polisiɲɛmɔgɔ, Sɛbɛn Cheru, y’a barika k’u sen don baaraw la, viziyokɔnferansi la, Mahamati Salɛhi Annadifu, Diɲɛtɔnba Sekeretɛri zenerali tɔgɔlamɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen, y’a fɔ a ɲɔgɔnye kɔfɛ, a ka ɲɔgɔnye kɔfɛ, ko « nin y’a san duuru ye ko ne bɛ SEYSIYA la ani nin y’a si
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko diɲɛmɔgɔ bɛ lahidu ta Mali la an’a bɛ prête ka Mali bilasira nin dakun kura la wa danaya don min na, danaya politiki yɛrɛ min bɛ yen, min bɛ yɛrɛ yɛrɛla’a fɔ.
Min ye Kolonɛli - mazɔri Isimayɛli Wage ye, Jamana bɛnɲini minisiri ye dantigɛ k’a fɔ ko « mɔgɔ bɔra fɔlɔ, danaya bɔra fɔlɔ dɔw la, danaya bɛ ka faamuya dɔw la,
Ola, Jɔdaba y’a jira k’a fɔ ko lajɛra ko Mali fan dɔ bɛ na to danayaw ɲɛtaabolo la ni waleyaw ye, ka taa la lakana koɲɛw kan ani ka ɲɛsin bolimafɛn ma min sɔrɔla bɛnkansɛbɛn na, walasa an ka segin ka tɛmɛ nin koɲɛ kan, ni ka dɛmɛ kɛ gɛlɛyaw ye bɛɛjɛlajɛlen fɛ ».
Mohamɛdi Lamini Ulidi Siddat fɛ, SEMA perezidan, « an ye baara kɛ Malidenw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A labɛnni kɛra ni Kidali marabolo gɔfɛrɛnɛri ye, wa Malidenw de ye nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛ labɛn, an tun ye min labaarali kɛ ɲɔgɔn fɛ ».
« SEYSIYA sigilen don yɔrɔ fɔlɔ ye, nin laadaltɔn Kidali marabolo kɔnɔ, siga t’a la, nin bɛnɲini, bɛnɲini, bɛnɲini Mali denw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Nin waatilabaara ye bɛɛ lajɛlen ye ko bɛɛ latigɛlen bɛ ɲɔgɔn fɛ Mali la », Basala Agi Hamzatta, bɛnkansɛbɛn kumalasela ye o fɔ.
« Ka Mali bandari ye fini bɔli la Kidali dugu kɔnɔ, o ye dusukasi ye an ye, o ye sebagaya ye an bolo.
Malidenw bɛɛ bɛ nin walejugu laɲini makɔnɔ Mali kɔnɔn, » Kolonɛli Modibo Kone, Mali lakana ani fasodenya minisiri,
SEYSIYA ka laadaltɔnsigi ka kan ka kɛ DEDEYRI taabolo taabolo la, fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaw sennateliya, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla,
An ka hakilijigin kɛ ko, Jamana ka dusukunjɛkulu fanba fanba bɛ Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn kama kalan kura na.
Berehima Jalo - Jamana ntolatannaw bɛ na ntolatan tako filanan an’a laban ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛ FIFA ka don senfɛ ( zuwɛn 2021 ) ni Tinizi ye.
A ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bɛ na kɛ taratadon zuwɛnkalo tile 15, Rabade Siti ntolatanyɔrɔ la,
O ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn jirala ka taa ni Kameru arbitrajɛkulu ka jɛkulu ye.
Jalatigɛla cɛmancɛkɔfɛjɔ, Ibarahima Nɔrɔdi, bɛna kɛ a fasodenw tɔgɔ, a ma, Ahmɛda Tawakisi ani Hani Abdelɛlatahɛ, dɛmɛni kama.
Jalatigɛla min bɛna kɛ, o bɛna kɛ ni Nizɛri Buali ye.
Ntolantan kɔfɛ Alɛri (0-1), zuwɛnkalo tile 6 tɛmɛnen, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kuncɛli la ride Kɔngo ( 1 – 1 ), Tumɛn, Mali Samatasɛgɛw bɛ ɲini ka dɛmɛ kɛ sababu ye k’u bɛn Tunikɛlaw ma.
Mohamɛdi Magasuba ka cɛw tɛ sira wɛrɛ sɔrɔ ni sebagaya ye.
Nin ntolatan senfɛ, Tinizi bɛna kɛ ntolatanna mɔgɔ caman bolo, i n’a fɔ Yusɛfu Maki, Ferjani Sasi, Dylani Bronn walima Wahbi Khari.
Wɛrɛ tɛmɛnen, Samatasɛgɛw ye ntolatan nul la ride Kɔngokaw ka Léopardɔmu (1-1).
A bilalen kɔfɛjɔyɔrɔ dɔ la, k’a da a la mɔgɔ jɔlenw kɔnɔ, FISE Nantes tɔgɔlatikɛla, Kalifa Kulibali, tun bɛ ɲɛsinnen do Awilew ka kurudon sɔrɔ (4nan ).
A labɛnnen kɛcogoya la, jamana ntolatannaw ye ntolatan ta domini la, nk’a ma se ka dɔ fara a ɲɔgɔn kan.

SEYSIYA ka ɲɔgɔnye bɛ bilasira Bamakɔ la, o kɛra Afiriki ni Erɔpu jamanaw cɛ depitebulon caman na, minnu faralenw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw dɔlakelen, i n’a fɔ Faransi ani Lamerikɛnjamana cɛ, o n’a kɔrɔtalen ye SEYSIYA ka ɲɔgɔnye tako duuruna kɛ Mali la, nka SEYSIYA ka nin ɲɔgɔnye tako 5nan ye Faransi minisiri ka senkɔrɔtalen ye, min y’a kɛ ye ni visiyokɔnferansi ye ani min ye SEYSIYA ka nin ɲɔgɔnye tako fɔlɔ kofɔ Kidali

Usumani M. Tarawore - Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye Bedegɔlidi kɛlɛde ye, a ka ɲɛmɔgɔ fɛ Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ ka fɔ la, Wɛrizali Bili Litili, ka fɔ la.
BedeGɔlidi Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ, Wɛrɛli Bili Litili, n’a ka baarakɛjama ye kunnafonodi lajɛba kɛ, zuwɛnkalo tile 14, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda ka daga la, walasa ka san 2020 kalo lataa ɲɛ, k’a ɲɛsinnenw ma yann’a ka ko nataw dantigɛ.
Bili Litili ka fɔ la, sɔrɔko sebagaya ɲɛnen san 2020 na, nafa sera a baarasigi waaribɔlaw ani fan caman mɔgɔ wɛrɛ minnu bɛ Mali la, a y’o dantigɛ.
BedeGɔlidi ye Sefa wari miliyari 34 ye saraw ani hadamadenya nafamafɛnw na, 162 di gɔfɛrɛnaman ye, 2,1 jate sigida jɛrɛjɛkuluw ka yiriwalinafolobɔ miliyari 82 ye.
San 2020 kɔnɔ, Fekola daman ye sanu ɔnsi 622 000 bɔ.
San 2021 kalosaba fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola daman tɛmɛna a ka sebagayaw waleyaliw ɲumanw fɛ, ni sanu ɔnsi 125 088 bɔli ye, k’a bɛn 7% ( 8 676 ) ma, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛsigilen kan.
San 2021 kɔnɔ, Fekola daman tun ka kan ka sanu ɔnsi bɔ k’a ta 530 000 ka taa 560 000 cɛ, minnu bɔli musakaw b’a ta Lamerikɛn dolariwari 405 ka taa 445 la ɔnsi kelen ani waribɔta kuurukaara ( RIPEYMU ) comprise entre 745 ka taa 785 la ɔnsi kelen.

Kasoka Dunbiya - Wankuwɛri ( Kanada ) Bedegolidi ( / B2Goligi ) ka jamanaw cɛ perezidandankan, Bili Litili, bɛ Bamakɔ, ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔya cakɛda daminɛ, kabini Mohamɛdi Jara ka baarabila, mɛkalo tile 17 laban na, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw dili saratilako kɔrɔ.
BedeGɔlidi – Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ kura ye kunnafonidilajɛ sigi, nin ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 14, lajɛrɛ sigi.
-maliweb.net – A ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn diyagoya la ni kunnafonidilaw ye, minnu ka laɲini ye ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda ka baarakɛlenw jira kabini a sigili.
Nka, donkibaruw, min sirilen don Manankoto yɔrɔ fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn dili kura mankan na, kɛra kumaw kɔnɔ.
ɛmɔgɔ ka kumafow la, k’a kɔdon a fɛn min bɛ yamaruya kɔnɔ, BedeGɔlidi Mali ma wari sɔrɔ k’a sababu kɛ Manankoto yamaruyasɛbɛnbɔli kɛli ye.
Lajɛ kumakɛla ka fɔ la, Manankoto yɔrɔ, Keɲeba fɛ, fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn sɔrɔla ale ka baarada fɛ san 2012 dugujukɔrɔfɛnw sariyasun sigibaju kan.
Nka, san 2019 dugujukɔrɔfɛnw sariyasun sigibaju de kan Dugujukɔrɔfɛnw minisiri ye fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn di kokura.
K’o kɛ, Bedegɔlidi kɛlen kɔ ka sɔn fɛn wajibiyalenw bɛɛ ma, gɔfɛrɛnaman fɛ, n’a ta bɛɛ.
Ne yɛrɛbakun ka gɛlɛya si t’anw ni minisiri cɛ.
Bili Litili y’o dantigɛ.
Nka, ɲɛmɔgɔ b’a jate ko marako gɛlɛya dɔ na se ka kɛ yen.
Kiritigɛbulonba minɛnen.
Mohamɛdi Jara ka baarabila kan, ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ b’a jate k’a ye baarabila kɛ a yɛrɛ ma.
A ko cogoya tun ka goni, o la, a ye baara bila bɛɛ ka hɛrɛ kama.
Barujigi kura y’o sɛmɛntiya.
Bi, Manankoto yamaruyasɛbɛn gafe bɛ Kiribulonba ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Bedegɔlidi k’a laɲini ka latigɛlisɛbɛn ta k’a sɔrɔbaga kura ka baaraw dulon, ma lamɛn Kiribulon mɔgɔw fɛ.
An bɛ kiri jaabi makɔnɔ a kɔnɔkow kan.
Bili y’o dantigɛ, min tɛ bɔli kɛ diɲɛ kiritigɛlaw ma, n’o ka kan.
Mamadu TOGOLA / maliweb.net - Kumalaseli min kɛra Buguni Urubaki Mayɛri (SUBE) fɛ, k’a daminɛ zanwiyekalo tile 1ɔlɔ k’a se desamburu tile 31 san 2019 ma, ko segin tɛ min na.
Komini tɔn ka kulusigi gabeya ye nafolomɔgɔ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ bin kɛra, san fila kɔnɔ, sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 208 na ( SEFAWARI 152 817 ) ma, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw kɔnɔ.
Minisiri Mamuru Kulibali bɛ na gɛlɛya.

O jɛɲɔgɔnjuguw fana.
A bɛ nɔ bɔ!
Bi, anw y’a maloya k’a fɔ ko anw ye Buguni Mayɛri tɔnw ye.

Fan bɔ minnu kɔnɔ, ni dɔwɛrɛyɔrɔw bɔli ye Minisiri baarakɛla ka baara la.
K’a bɔ ɲɔgɔna sariyaw la, minnu tɛ dabila ka laban ka bɔ sigida tɔn kɔnɔ.
Dɛmɛbaw ani ninjuguw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen, bɔlɔlɔ baarabodatigi dɔ bɛ Buguni Komini Urubaha ka baara lataa, nin kumaw fɛ, a ka mara ɲɛnabɔcogo tiɲɛni kan.

An ka kunnafonisunw ka fɔ la, Buguni mɛri bɛ mankun na.

Fɔlɔ, ɲɛnabɔcogo jugu.

Wa bi, ni pisi in kɛra ɲɔgɔn ye.
Kow tiɲɛni magoɲɛw kɔnɔ. K’a daminɛ zanwiye 2017 la ka taa bila san 2019 la, an ɲɔmɔgɔw b’a ɲɛfɔ, k’a bɔ u ka mɔgɔlaɲini, Buguni meri Mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali, an’a ka kulu ye sabanan ye, min kɛra gabegie ye.
Sɛbɛnw kɔnɔ, baarabodatigi dɔ bɛ ɲɛfɔli kɛ Minisiri kɔlɔsilikɛdaga ka kɔlɔsilikɛyɔrɔ la.
A bɛ fara a kan, fɛn minnu tilennen don ka bɔ DAWO ( Kunnafonidisɛbɛn kunbɛnw ) fɛ, ka se se sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 950 000 ma ani kalandenkɔrɔw sarali, minnu ma dɔrɔmɛ, Bugunikaw ka Komini kɔnɔ, ka se sefawari miliyon 126,7 hakɛ ma ( sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 676 ).
Foco wɛrɛw, minnu sirilen don Buguni meri ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, jantolantɛmɛnw sirabakan sarati jɔnjɔn kan, ka se se sefawari miliyon 53 ma ( sefawari miliyon 10 ) ani saraliw kɛ kasɔrɔ siga t’a la, ka se se sefawari miliyon 10 ma ( sefawari miliyon 11 ).
Wa, min bɛ tila, an ka kunnafonisunw ka fɔ la, o ye ko Buguni mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali, bɛ nafaw lamɛn, minnu kɛra sefawari miliyon 3,8 ye (3 875 000).
Bɛɛ bɔlen kɔ yen, Buguni Mayɛri baarakɛlaw y’a dajira ko dɔwɛrɛw, minnu bɛ kɛlen don yɛrɛkofɔbaara baara la, bɛ sariyasigiba ani sariyalakotigiba kɔnɔ.
A bɛ don nafolokow siratigɛ la, nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli kɔnɔ.
Anw ka kumaɲɔgɔnw ka ɲɛfɔ ko Minisiri ɲɛmɔgɔya fan caman tɛ u ka jɔyɔrɔw ni u ka jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw la, fɛn min bɛ kɛ minnu na ni jaabi minnu sɔrɔlenw ye ɲɛbila.
O la, fɛnw kɛlen kɔ, minnu sirilen bɛ fasodensow hadamadenya marali ɲɛmɔgɔya la, bɛ bugɔempêche ka Buguni meri kɛ ka ɲɛtaa ni ɲuman ye fasodensow ka baaraw lasegin.
Min ye domaniale ani nafoloko ɲɛnabɔcogo kan, anw ka kunnafoniw b’a jira k’a fɔ ko Buguni Mayɛri ma kɛ waleyaw kɛ minnu ka kan k’u ka laɲiniw ɲɛnabɔ cogo min, n’u ka kan ka jaabiw kɛ minnu dira a ma, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, kunnafoni ni fasodenw bɛɛ ɲɛnabɔcogo ɲuman ye bolofaraw cɛmancɛli la.
A laselikɛla baarakɛlaw promotion taabolo sennateliyali bɛ SUBE baarakɛjama ka wale labɛn kologɛlɛya.
Wa bi, baarakɛminɛnw ni baarakɛmatɛmɛw, i n’a fɔ cogo min bɛ yen Buguni Mayɛri la, tɛ ɲɛnamaya la, k’a sababu kɛ gafew dɔgɔyali ma, walasa ka baarakɛminɛnw lasɔrɔli an’u sendon.
Ka da an kumamɔgɔw ka dantigɛliw la an ka kumaɲɔgɔnw la, Buguni yɛrɛmarakafo ka kolatigɛjɛkulu ye nafamafɛnw sɔrɔ minnu dira Mɛtiri Mamuru Kulibali ma, sigidajama kolatigɛkulu mɔgɔw ye, ani fɛɛrɛw kɛ baaradaba dɔw la, minnu bɔra Jamana kɔnɔ.
An ka kunnafonisunw b’an hakililatigɛ.
Buguni mɛri la, Farikoloɲɛnacɛkɛ ye dantigɛli kɛ ko Komini jɛkulu bɛ nafaw sɔrɔ, minnu bɛ dɛmɛ kɛ, dɛmɛli kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw na ani dɛmɛli kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw sarali ye.
Awɛnw kɛcogoyaw bénéficianw ye,
Mɛri, sigidajamaw ka biro mɔgɔw, sigidaw ka ciyakɛda baarakɛlaw ani baarakɛjɛkulu baarakɛkuluw mɔgɔw.
Yaan’a kɛ pereperelatigɛ.
San 2010 zuwɛnkalo tile 28 Dantigɛlisɛbɛn n°005 / SEYBE bilali la, Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ye san 2017 mɛkalo tile 29 Dantigɛlisɛbɛn n°06 / SUBE ta, min bɛ tali kɛ Marawisar ani Billeteura la, n’a bɛ ɲini ka Minisiri ka dɛmɛ ɲɛmɔgɔyasɛbɛn kɔnɔbaara kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen kelen tali kama.
O la, a b’a lase sefawari dɔrɔmɛ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 25 000 ma, min bɛ nafolo bɔli kama ani sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 50 000, k’a ɲɛsin Mɛri ka saratiw ani talifoni ma.
A dun tɛ, o nafaw tɛ prévun ka kɛ a baarasariya la, min bɛ senna.
Wari hakɛ bakuruba, min saratiwaati saratiwaati kɔnɔ, tɛmɛna kɛra sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 25 000 (miliyon mugan ni wolonwula ani ba bi segin ni wolonwula ) ma.
A bɛ damatɛmɛ sariya la. O bɔlen kɔ yen, anw ka kunnafonisunw b’a fara a kan ko Buguni Mayɛri Sɛbɛnnikɛlaba ma wari minnu sɔrɔla foroba cakɛdaw (DAWO) la.
An ka sefawari miliyon 1,8 kɔnɔ ( sefawari miliyon 1 170 000 ), sɛgɛsɛgɛli cakɛda ma sɔrɔ ko segin tɛ sefawari miliyon 900 000 hakɛ kan.
Wari min bɔra o wari hakɛ la o kɛra sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 490 000 ye.
Wa o tɛ tɛmɛnen don.
Ka caya,
Hali ni bugunikaw ka mɛri Mamuru Kulibali tɛ ladiyalifɛnw kɛcogoyaw lataa ɲɛ, minnu waleyali bɛ ka dɔgɔfiyɛ la.
O cogo la, mɔgɔ minnu ye suguw n°046 / SUBE – DRIPEYMU – SIK 2018 kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye, min bɛ tali kɛ kalansɛyɔrɔ ba fila ( 3 ) sɔrɔ,
Biro-magasi équipée, lakanabaarako fila ( 2 ) kɔnɔ, Jalanikoro, Heremakono Nɔgɔdanfɛ, Buguni komini Urubaki kɔnɔ.
ani n°047 / SUBE - DMUYSI - SIK 2018, min bɛ tali kɛ Dugunikaw, Heremakono Cɛmancɛw ka yamaruyasɛbɛnw kɛyɔrɔw la ani Masakakura Komini Urubakiw ka SEWODEYSICOMW, min bɛ Funankɛnɛya yɔrɔ la, ye bolonɔbila kɛ waatiw saratiw ma kasɔrɔ Minisiri Mamuru ma tileniyabaara kɛ a ma.
Nin sariyaw minnu tɛmɛna lawaliya la, bɛ na jate sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 8 142 830 (miliyon mugan ni wolonwula ani ba mugan ni bi segin ni wolonwula ani kɛmɛ ni bi segin ni bi saba) la.
O waati kɔnɔ, an ka kunnafonisunw b’a jira k’a fɔ ko sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛkulu ye baarakɛminɛnw labaaraliw sɛgɛsɛgɛli, minnu bɛ tali kɛ wari, wusuruw ani baarakɛtaw kan Buguni Komini Urubaki kɔnɔ, forobasɛbɛnw, saratiw ani jurudon talenw kan.
A ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw kɔnɔ, a bɛ ye ko nafolokow baarakɛjɛkulu perezidan ye yamaruyasɛbɛnw kɛ, minnu bɛ bila ka taa Régisɛri yɛrɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, k’a kɛ dugujukɔrɔfɛnw loyɛliw ye.
O de la, waati kɔnɔ min sen bɔra sen na, nafolowari hakɛ bakuruba ye sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 5 760 000 ye, min donnen don haliliw kama, baarakɛjɛkulu perezidan, min bɛ nafolowari ɲɛsinnen don, ye sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 650 000 hakɛ sɔrɔ a ma, o kɔfɛ, ye sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 1 159 000 hakɛ sɔrɔ, sɛbɛnfuraɲɛ kelen ka nɔfɛ filɛli kɔfɛ.
Wari hakɛ kɛlenw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw, minnu sɔrɔla baarakɛjɛkulu Perezidan fɛ, ka ca n’a ye miliyon 4 ye (4 170 000).
montagew grotesquesow. Kow cayali, min bɛ bɔ Buguni Mayiri la, bɛ tɛmɛnni kɔnɔ.
O la, an ɲɔmɔgɔw b’a ɲɛfɔ ko Buguni Akademi dɛmɛni ɛmɔgɔba ye kalanw kofɔ, minnu bilalen don k’u bolo, ni Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ka latigɛli ye kalanw salenw ye Buguni Komini Urubaki kɔnɔ.
O cogo la, sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛlakulu y’a lakɔlɔsi ko, k’a da saraw cogoyaw kan, minnu sɔrɔla kalanso Lajɛba fɛ, Buguni meri, Mamuru Kulibali, ye saraw doniw saraliw cakɛdaw saraliw saraliw ta a ka Komini kɔnɔ kasɔrɔ sarati hukumu kɔnɔn.
A wari hakɛ jateminɛlen, a waati kɔnɔ, sɔrɔli tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ, ka ca ni an ka sefawari miliyon 126 ye ( SEFAWARI 130 ).
Wa sɔrɔ nafoloko ɲɛnabɔli kama, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla baarakɛkulu y’a da kɛnɛ kan ko Buguni meri Sariyasɛbɛnw bɛ jateminɛ kofɔlen ɲɛnabɔli sarati wajibiyalen kan, min lakodɔnnen don kɛnɛ kan waati min kɔnɔ.
O la, sɛgɛsɛgɛlimakɛlaw ka fɛsɛgɛsɛgɛliw, yɛlɛmasɛgɛw, yɛlɛmasɛgɛw ka yɛlɛmasɛgɛsɛgɛw, ani wari hakɛw, minnu bɛ tali kɛ yɛrɛyɛrɛw la, bɔlen b’a fɛ ko Buguni Mayɛri Régisɛri ye wari hakɛ caman kofɔ, k’a sababu kɛ yɛrɛyɛrɛ kofɔlenw kofɔlenw ye.
Marajɛkuluw hakɛ bakuruba, min bɛ tali kɛ, san 2018 ani san 2019 baarawaati kɔnɔ, jate waribɔlɔw cɛ jate ani wari hakɛ minnu donna a baaraɲɔgɔnna ma, kɛra sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 24 087 130 (miliyon mugan ni wolonwula ani ba bi segin ni wolonwula ani kɛmɛ ni bi saba) la.
I n’a fɔ o tun tɛ bɔli kɛ, yamaruyasɛbɛn wɛrɛw dilannamɔgɔw bolo, san 2018 ani san 2019 kɔnɔ, wari hakɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ baliya ma kɛ a wari hakɛ miliyon 29 ye ( SEFAWARI 10 000 ).
Wari hakɛ kɛlenw tɛmɛnenw bɛ jate kɛ sefawari miliyon 53,9 ye ( sefawari miliyon 53 999 750 )
K’a kɛ dɔrɔn, san 2017 kɔnɔ, ɲɛkɔrɔw tilaliw kofɔlenw na, ɲɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla ye wari miliyon 10 sɔrɔ ( sefawari 400 ) ma, siga t’a la, ni sariyasɔsɔli ye.
Sigida yiriwali kologɛlɛn senfɛ. Ka tɛmɛ nin nafoloko caman kunfɛjɔyɔrɔw fɛ, Buguni Komini Urubaki Mayɛri ka kɛsuw, ye Sefa wari miliyon 208 hakɛ kɛ ( Sefa wari miliyari 143 817 ) wajibiya, anw ɲɔmɔgɔw y’o pereperelatigɛ.
Min ye mangekarati gɛlɛya ye bugunikamarafogon na ye, o ye Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ka ban jira k’a ka laadalaɲɔgɔnye kɛsɛbɛnw rendua public la.
O cogo de la, olu y’a jira k’a fɔ ko mɛri ye PEDEYASIK (Perezidan wote ka sɔrɔko ani hadamadenyako yiriwali baarabolofara yiriwali ) kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu sigi,
Yaan’a k’a fara a kan k’a bɛ suguyaw dilannen ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
ani a tɛ fɛ ka Komini ka ɲɛfɔliw sɛgɛsɛgɛliw lafisaya.
O ɲɛnabɔcogo jugu kɔfɛ, an ka kunnafonisunw b’a da kɛnɛ kan ko Buguni Mayɛri tɛ mɔgɔ ye.
Minisiri ɲɛmɔgɔ, Mamuru Kulibali, ka kumakanw ye foroba ɲɛmɔgɔ ye, minnu kɔrɔkow bɛ foroba ɲɛmɔgɔ ye.
Gansan fana, yɛrɛkofɔ ni ɲɔgɔnfaamuyako la, minnu bɛ lagosi a ɲɛfɛ gestion fɛ.
Buguni dugubakɔnɔmɔgɔw ka ko juguw bɛ sɔrɔ ni mansi peu de kɔnɔ.
Marakofɛnw kɛcogoya, nafolo bɔli kɛrɛfɛ ani mɔgɔ ressourcesow ani nafolo bɔli kɛli mankanba la.

Zan Piyɛri Jimitɛri - Jamana Mara ani Cakɛda Minisiri, kuntigi kɔrɔ Abudulayi Mayiga, ye donba, alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 29, san 2021, Bamakɔ Foroba lajɛba yɔrɔ la, a baarakɛatelier ka kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen pe mara san 2021 kalatabaaraw waatiw la.
A bɛ kɛbagaw bɛɛlajɛlen (Administration, Politikiw la, Jɛrɛjɛkuluw la, Mara kɔnɔmɔgɔw, Dɔgɔtɔrɔw la )ma.
Fɔlɔ bɛna kɛ mɔgɔ minnu sen bɛ a la, baaraw daminɛ senfɛ, ka bɛnkansɛbɛn laban sɔrɔ min na, a bɛ se ka kɛ sababu ye ka kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen pe labɛn, kalataw caman minnu ɲɛsigilen don Cɛmancɛlafanga kɔnɔ.
Hakili jigin na, Abudulayi Mayiga y’a da tulow kan ko kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen pe dama de tun tɛ bɔ cɛmancɛlafanga sariyaw sɔrɔ, nk’a bɛ ye Jamana Kumaɲɔgɔnya Bɛɛ sen bɛ min na komagɛlɛyali ta ye.
O kosɔn, Kolonɛli Abudulahi Mayiga, Premieriɲɛmɔgɔ, Gɔfɛrɛnaman kuntigi, ye kumalaseli dakun lakuraya, walasa k’a ɲini k’a fɔ ko Cɛmancɛlafanga kalata nataw labɛnnen bɛ se ka kɛ yen, kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen pe labɛnnen ye.
O de kosɔn, minisiri Mayiga y’o fara a kan, a kɛra ko a ka baaradaba ka fɛn kun ye ka politikitɔnw ani jɛrɛjɛkuluw ka fɔtaw sɔrɔ a koɲɛ kan.
A kofɔlen tɔn, a ko ten, b’a latigɛ nin hukumu kɔnɔ.
Walasa ka hakililadi politikitɔnw kan a koɲɛ kan, baaraw daminɛ senfɛ, Abudulayi Mayiga y’a dajira ko labɛnnen fila, bɛna kɛ.
A fɔlɔ bɛ taamasiyɛn kow cogoya kan, k’a da kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen kan ( Jamana Mara ani Cakɛda Minisiriso ).
A filanan bɛ taabolo lakɔlɔsi kan, min bɛ tali kɛ kalataw labɛnni kan Cɛmancɛlafanga kɔfɛ, Mali kɔnɔ ( Jamana koɲɛnabɔlaw minnu bɛ minnu na ).
A sabanan bɛ tali kɛ kalataw ɲɛnabɔcogow ta Mali kɔnɔ, kalata nataw labɛnniw an’u cɛsirikow, minnu bɛ na kɛ kalataw ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛmɔgɔyabulon kelen bolo, min bɛ se ka bila sen kan ( Jamana ).
FIli laban na, a bɛ taabolo lakɔli yamaruya, fɛɛrɛw, minnu ka kan ani waati min ka kan, kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen pe labɛnni kama kalata nataw labɛnni kama ani sirakunw, minnu bɛ se ka kɛ sariyasɔsɔli kɛbagaya kama (Dɔgɔtɔrɔba min bɛ kalataw la ).
O kɔfɛ, minisiri Abudulayi Mayiga y’a jira k’a fɔ ko kumafalenw kɔfɛ, kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kannabilalen kelen pe marako bɛɛ sen na.
Ne tun tɛ se ka galabu kɛ kasɔrɔ fɛɛrɛkow ani nafolokow boloɲɔgɔnmaw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ani fangabulonw bɛɛ fo u ka kɔkɔrɔdon ani bilasirali la an ka jamana lakana, lakana ani yiriwali la, a y’a kuncɛ ten.
Hadama B. Fofana - A seginnen a ka dugunin na Mama ka dugunin kɔnɔ, Konowari woroduguyanfan cɛmancɛ la, perezidan kɔrɔ Loran Bagibo ye a ka kiritigɛli fɔ, ntɛnɛdon, diɲɛ kirisoba ka fɔ la.
« Ne tɛ mɔgɔ jalakilen ye ». Nin y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye kabini a seginnen Konowari, perezidan kɔrɔ Loran Bagibo kumana, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28 don, a ka kiritigɛli an’a ka bilali diɲɛ kojugu Kiriso (SEPEYI) la, k’a sɛmɛntiya ko a tun bilala ka taa Lahayi, bawo « tun ka kan ka cɛ mankutulen dɔgɔya ».
« SESPEYI, o tun tɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛli ɲɛ, fo mɔgɔ min tun ka kan ka bɔ cɛ mankan, o tuman na a y’i dogo », Loran Bagibo y’o dantigɛ Mama ka sonyali la, Konowari woroduguyanfan cɛmancɛ la.
Nka, a y’a fara a kan, ka sin laadaw ɲɛmɔgɔw, a ka paritiɲɛmɔgɔw ani kunnafonidilaw ma, « ne ka nimisa t’a la, k’a da a kan n tun bɛ taga i n’a fɔ n tun bɛ ɲanamaya tɔgɔtigiya sɔrɔ, aw bɛɛ de ye minnu fɛ ».
Loran Bagibo laban ka jalatigɛ, marisikalo laban, SEYNIPE fɛ, yɔrɔ min na a jalaki tun bɛ kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲiniw ɲɛkɔrɔ, n’o kɛra sababu ye a segin ka na Konowari.
« Ganti minnu t’an dɔn, minnu b’an ka ŋanayaɲiniw ɲɛfɛ, minnu b’an fara ɲɔgɔn kan sisan, y’a dɔn k’an ( tun tɛ ).
N bɛ fɛn bɛɛ kɛ, nka n tɛ jalakibaga ye », Loran Bagibo y’o kɛ sɛmɛntiyali kɔnɔ.
A tun bɛ kumaɲɔgɔnya kɛ tuman dɔ la ni ladalaɲɛmɔgɔw ye minnu bilalen bɛ ɲɔgɔn kan u kɔnɔn, minnu suguyaw ye dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan, minnu bɔra a ka cɛmancɛkɔrɔ fan bɛɛ la, n’u y’a ka « bɛnɲini » ci ta.
« bɛnɲini damatɛmɛ » « a tun ye mɔgɔ min na ka bɛn sɔrɔ bɛnɲini kama.
Fo k’a jɔ k’a kan to a ka mɔgɔya jɔyɔrɔ la yaasa ka Konowari fasojama wele bila bɛɛ laɲini totale ma », Zan Goli Obu, Mama ka « sɛnɛw « ɲɛmɔgɔ, sigida fanga « ɲɛmɔgɔ, n’o ye notablew ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Nin jamanakuntigisariyaw ka kan fana k’u sen don a ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ dɔ la min ka laɲini b’a kɛ « hakililatigɛ », i n’a fɔ a ka jamana ka danaya b’a yɛrɛ minɛ ka bila kaso la ani ka bila kaso la.
« Mardi, n bɛna a lasegin, n bɛna a ɲini a fɛ ko bɛnɲini ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛmɔgɔya la, a k’a ka kuma fɔlɔw nationi na ka taa bɛnɲini sira taabolo la », « dugukolo ɲɛmɔgɔw » y’o sɛmɛntiya, k’a sɛmɛntiya k’a ka ciyakɛdaw ciyakɛdaw tali ye nin ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ kɔnɔ.
« Jamana béte la, ni denbaya mɔgɔ bɔlen bɛ na gɛlɛya cogoya gɛlɛman kɔnɔ, an b’a ladiyali kɛ.
O kɛra ye ka ɲɛbila a ka sojɔyɔrɔ la sɔgɔmada nɛgɛ ɲɔgɔn kan sɔgɔmada fɛ, ni ramɛw ani feuillew tun bɛ ɲɛ Kpobra ani Tita la ɲumanw ye », a ɲɛmɔgɔba y’o ɲɛfɔ.
Mama ka foroba yɔrɔ la, dugudenw y’u makɔnɔn dɔrɔn, n’u dansɛ ani n’u mankan kɛ, perezidandan kɔrɔ bɛ k’u kumakan kɔrɔ.
« Bagibo bɔra ka bɛn matarafali di jamana kɔnɔ », Bɛnbi Kudu y’a ɲɛfɔ, min kɔrɔlen don Zebizeku dugunin kɔnɔ.
« Ne nisɔndiyalen don, nin don ye koɲɛ ye.
Perezidan Bagibo kannabila.
Mɔgɔ b’a la fɔ, a bɛ fɔ durɔn kelen kan », Beratrice Jɛje, min bɔra Kpaku, y’o dantigɛ, k’a bɛn « bɛn ani bɛnɲini » ta bolo la, senkɔrɔmadon na.
Mɔgɔba ba caman y’a bisimilali ɲuman di Mama ma, tile tan kɔfɛ a seginnen ka na Abidjan.
Segin ka na gɛlɛya si ma kɛ, k’a sɔrɔ a ka natɔn ɲɔgɔn fɛ a ka bɔli ye zuwɛnkalo tile 17 Abijan, marquée ni mɔgɔsira caman wulikajɔ ye lakanatigilamɔgɔw ni lakanakɛbagaw cɛ, minnu tun bɛ fɛ k’a wele bila a ka bandari pankurunnin na.
Loran Bagibo, to fanga sɔrɔ kabini 2000 la, tun minɛna awirili 2011 Awirikan, k’a bila kalo wɔɔrɔ senfɛ ka taa Sepiki la yaasa ka kiri ɲangiliw kɛli kɔ kɔfɛ san 2010 perezidansigikalata laban na.
A ka ban k’a ka faamuya sɔrɔ ka ɲɛsin Alasani Watara ma, o tun ye kalafili kɔ gɛlɛyaba ye min ye mɔgɔ 3 000 ye.
A latigɛlen san 2020 ɔkutɔburukalo la sabanan sabanan na, laban ni sabanan sabanan ye, Alasani Watara y’a yamaruya di Loran Bagibo seginni kɔfɛ, tile damadɔ o kɔfɛ.
SUN : FRANCE 24 - Perezidan Habibu Sisoko ka jagokɛla bakurubafeerekɛbagaw daminɛna jumadon, ka tɛmɛ « Liberason » kunnafonidisɛbɛn dɔ fɛ, min y’a ka dɛmɛ kumakɛɲɔgɔn kan, min bisigilen don « waridun caman » ( Habibu t’a labila ka ɲɛsin nin titre ma, a bɛ i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ b’a m’i miiri ko n’a tun bɛ nin magotɛgɛ ɲɔgɔn na, an tun bɛ na kuma fɔ a yɛrɛ kan cogo min).
Min ye sɛgɛsɛgɛliw ye, o ye labɛn kura autour dɔ ka kɛɲɛ ni laselisɛbɛn dɔ ye ( an bɛn min fɔ a ma waati opportunon na ) Jamana nafoloko kunnafonisɛbɛnw ( Setifɛn ) bolofara kɔnɔ.
Ka tɛmɛ a kɛnɛ kan, k’a fɔ cogoya la, fɛn don min bɛ kɛ ka perezidan Habibu Sisoko nimisa.
Munna?
N’a ɲini k’a fɔ mɔgɔ minnu tɛ fɛ k’o danayaba ani hakililatigɛba ye, min bɛ Mali ka ɲɛtaaɲɛ jɔ farikoloɲɛnajɛ la ani kɛrɛfɛtigi ye majɛ kɔnɔ.
Anw tɛ fɛ ka dɔgɔtɔrɔ kɛ Dakari ( Senegali ) la, nka, anw bɛ se ka ɲɛfɔ k’a fɔ ko nin koɲɛ in ɲɛfɛla fa siɲɛ dɔgɔtɔrɔ, k’a da a kan Habibu ka nin ɲɛnamaya bɛ mɔgɔ dɔw jagoya ɲɔgɔn na.
Mɔgɔ kelen-kelen minnu tɛ jɔyɔrɔtigiw ye, minnu ye ko bɛɛ kɛ walasa ka Mali dankari fanga la ni tɔgɔlamɔgɔw fɛ.
Habibu kɛlen ni wasa sɔrɔli ye abada, a ma se k’i kɔrɔ.
Sɔsɔli tɛ yafa kɛ daliluw walima kunkow ye, walasa k’a tiɲɛ dafiriw kɔrɔ, minnu tun bɛ labɛnnen bɛɛ k’a ka ja in janto la, nka a ma deli k’i yɛrɛ di u dakun na.
A ye waati bɛɛ k’a ka baara kɛ, k’a da a kan a dalen b’a la ko n’u t’a fɔ k’a gɛlɛya foori kɔnɔ o y’a da a kan k’u vision ni baraka t’u bolo ka se ka jɔyɔrɔtigiya ɲɛtaa la.
I n’a fɔ a y’o adage kɛ, min b’a hakilijigin kɛ ko « kuma ye min bɛ boli tɔw la ».
ɲangili ma diya mɔgɔ lafaamuya.
Wa, nin mɔgɔ ɲangiliw tɛ dɔn ko ninnu ma dɔn, o ye k’a fɔ ko Sɔrɔ ɲɛmɔgɔ ma ɲini ka destini ɲɛgɛn, hali n’a y’a ka tɛmɛ tɛmɛ parcoursɛri kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye ani min lakodɔnnen bɛ a ka dusukunnako ni ɲɛmɔgɔya fɛ.
An ka fɔ la, a tɛ na Habibu Sisoko ani Hamani angi de ka lakana kɔnɔ, nka Mali ni jamana wɛrɛw bɛɛ de ka kan ka wulikajɔ kɛ o kama.
Ani k’o kɛ, k’a da a kan farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔba fila ninnu ye jamana lasigidenw ye, nka fana kun bɛɛ, k’a da a kan an bɛ sababu bɛ ye k’i miiri ko nin janfaw kɛ ka ɲɛsin u ma kɛnɛ kan.
Cogoya dɔ de tun bɛ kɛ jamana walima fanga dɔw ŋaniya ka bɔ an ka jamana lataaɲɛ fan wɛrɛ fɛ, min, fo yan, y’a jira k’a fɔ kunnafonidilaw ka lakodɔn, ola, jamana ɲɛ ye danaya ye.
An ka jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya tun ka kan ka kɛlɛli ɲɛbila sɛbɛnfuraɲɛ la min bɛ gɛlɛya kɔnɔ bawo farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɔdaw tɛ mɔgɔw ka don bi.
Farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɔyɔrɔw ka ɲɛna kosɛbɛ. O cogo la, kabini Alimpikiya yɛlɛmani la ka se sankɛmɛsariya kɔnɔ, Kuberɛtiba Baron Pɛri Piyɛri ka houlette la, farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɔyɔrɔ politiki ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ ma se ka dɔgɔya.
O de la,Nɛlisɔni Mandela (n’a bɛ daminɛ zuluyekalo tile 8 – 10 ), y’i kɔkɔrɔjigi bila irigibi kupudiɲɛni ma, walasa k’a ka jamana faraɲɔgɔnkan politiki lafinni na, walasa k’a ka jamana « Azimu ni tile » sigi.
« Farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɛra yɔrɔyakɛlɛmana source ye ani kumaɲɔgɔnya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye, n’o ye influence media ye.
Farikoloɲɛnajɛw bɛ sɛmɛntiya i n’a fɔ u ka jamana lasigidenw ye, dɔwɛrɛ caman dɔwɛrɛ ka tɛmɛ mɔgɔ wɛrɛ fɛ, minnu dɔnnen don hali n’a y’a sɔrɔ u yɛrɛ jamana kɔrɔ.
Mɔgɔ bɛ mɔgɔ kɛ Usain Bɔliti walasa Jamaikaw la walima Novak Jokovici walasa Serbiya », diɲɛmɔgɔ dɔ tun b’o kofɔ a ka diɲɛmɔgɔw ka laselisɛbɛn de kɔnɔ.
Mɔgɔ b’a faamuya o la, munna na fanga ɲɔgɔnw bɛɛ ka kɛbi walasa k’u yɛrɛ di farikoloɲɛnajɛ fɛɛrɛw ma.
Ani k’o kɛ, k’a da a kan « farikoloɲɛnajɛ bɛ diɲɛ ɲɔgɔndan sugu dɔ ye ».
An ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ jamana kɛ ka kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ jamana ye, i n’a fɔ an ɲɛmɔgɔw y’a fɔ k’a yɛrɛ firifiri, k’a bɛn a politiki, diplomatiki, diɲɛmɔgɔkow, dantigɛli, kan.
ani fana sɔrɔko
Nin kuncɛɲininkali kama, aw b’a jira k’a fɔ ko farikoloɲɛnajɛ sɔrɔ ye, ni Erɔwari miliyari 600 ye, k’a jate 2 % la, diɲɛ kɔnɔnasaadɛn (PIBE) hakɛ caman na.
Kabini a bɛ gɛlɛya suguya caman kɔnɔ kabini a ka ca ni san bi wɔɔrɔ tɛ, Mali nafa bɛ k’a jate ko farikoloɲɛnajɛ bɛ kɛ jamanaw cɛ boloda min bɛ se ka kɛ sababu ye k’a ka lataamani n’a ka diɲɛmɔgɔya lasegin.
O de b’a jira ko an ka kan ka Mali tɔgɔlamɔgɔ kura politiki kɛ diɲɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛw kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la latigɛli postew la.
Juguman na, fɛn bɛɛ bɛ kɛ bi k’an ka tɔgɔlamɔgɔw salire lajɛkulu dɔw la, k’a sababu kɛ tɔw ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw kunbɛn.
Ani k’o kɛ kasɔrɔ an ka jamanaw cɛsiri riposte b’a la i n’a fɔ a ka kan.
N’an y’a miiri yɛrɛ ye ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ jamana kɛ fitini ye, an tɛ se ka kɛ k’an diɲɛ fasodenw ma, minnu y’u ka kɛlɛ k’u ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkulu sigili la Afiriki ani diɲɛ fɛɛrɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw faraɲɔgɔnkan ɲɛmɔgɔya la, ni k’a ɲɔgɔn dafa Maliden wɛrɛw ka dɛmɛ jɛlenya kɔnɔ, hali n’a ɲɔgɔnna ma kɛ ten ani n’a ɲɔgɔnna Maliden tɔw ka dɛmɛ jɛlenya kɔnɔ, hali n’a ɲɔg
Mɔgɔ minnu bɛ nin cɛ in ɲɛmɔgɔya laɲumanba fɛ ani n’a kɛlenba ye, ka Habibu Sisoko jalaki ni nafolo kɛli ye, o ye sugolako ye, k’a da a kan a y’i tiɲɛ ka farikoloɲanajɛ kɛ, fɔlɔ la judo, o kɔfɛ ɲɔgɔndanbaliya, walasa ka farikoloɲanajɛ bolibagaw bila u ka ɲinifɛnw la.
Nka i n’a fɔ a m’a dabila nin mɔgɔ prochew la, a y’i yɛrɛ remisi Dia ma tuma bɛɛ.
O delina fana tɛ kɛ kɔfɛjɔ ɲuman ye kɔrɔfɛjɔ ɲuman ye, mɔgɔ min b’a ka sumaya lafasa tuma bɛɛ.
O cogo la, mɔgɔ t’a fɔ ko, « an bɛ se ka fɛn bɛɛ kɛ, an bɛ se ka fɛn bɛɛ kɛ.
nka ko bɛɛ tiɲɛ don.

Alisali ( Zuwɛnkalo tile 21 san 2021 kunnafonidisɛbɛn « U kɛra mun ye? » baara kolatigɛ la, kunnafonidisɛbɛn kɛcogoya hakilila bɛ héraw bɛɛ bolo.
Kabini a dayɛlɛnnen, a y’i sɛbɛntiya nin hukumu kɔnɔ yaasa ka cɛw ni musow bɔ minnu ye koɲɛ jateminɛ kɔnɔ.
Nka an ka kan fana ka mɔgɔ dɔw sɔrɔ u bɛɛ la, dɔw minnu bɛ baara ɲumanba kɛ ani cɛbɔli caman bɛ min kɔnɔ.
Nin ye an ka dɔgɔkun ŋanaŋana in ye, Usumani Jara, SEWOBE ntolatanna kɔrɔ, Bamakɔ disiriki tɔgɔla ligi kɔrɔ mɔgɔ kɔ, Fémafuti perezidan kɔrɔ, Afiriki Ntolatan Faraɲɔgɔnkankuluw ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw labɛnni jɔyɔrɔtigi kɔrɔ, Femafuti perezidan kɔrɔ, Dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, kɔlɔsili ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ,
Kumasurun na.
A ka dantigɛliw labɛnnen do bɛ minnu na, ni mago kɛli ye k’a ka faseri jateminɛ, o de kɛra an ma, walasa ka an mago ɲɔgɔn kɔrɔlenw dɔgɔya.
A ka bɔ Femmefiti ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ 1992 la, a sɔnna ka bɔ janama kɔnɔ, ka to farikoloɲɛnajɛ ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ fana kɔnɔ.
Anw sera ka Femafuti perezidan kɔrɔ nɔfɛ, kumalaseli dɔ fɛ, Bubakari M. Jalo, a bɛ fɔ min ma Sepp Mayi, jamana ntolatantɔnw jalatigi kɔrɔ an’a kine tɔgɔlamɔgɔw bɛɛ fɔ.
Ba Usumani ye an bisimila a ka cabinet la, a ka sogo kɔnɔ Bamakɔkura,
Usumani Jara bɛ dusu tiɲɛ na ntolatan kɔnɔ, k’a da a kan a y’a to a ka mɔgɔ caman ye an ka jamana kɔnɔ, Afiriki ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
Bi, a bɛ fɛn min dɔnnen don cɛw ani diɲɛ vie la, a ka kan ka kɛ ntolatan ye.
K’a kɛ i n’a fɔ n’a ɲɛmɔgɔ ye a ka dɛmɛ kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ baaraw la, a ka baara occupationw kɔnɔ, foroba ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, y’a to ka ntolatan kɛ nɔfɛ ni yɛlɛma ye, foyi si tɛ se ka kɛ min na.
Nka, Usumani Jara ka dɔgɔyalenbaw bɛ fɔɲɔgɔn juguw kɔnɔ ni tilennibaliya juguw ye, dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan an’a kɔrɔlɔbaw durɔn, wa kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, o minnu na, farikoloɲɛnajɛ bɛ se ka minɛ.
A ka fɔ la, cɛbɔ ni tɔn hakililatigɛ b’a sɔrɔ ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɛ a ka waati la, n’a kɛra ntolatanna ye.
A ni Usumani Jara ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛra sababu ye k’a ka kow ɲɛnabɔ.
Jamana cɛ kow ye, min b’a ban ka jatew ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ ni tariku sɛbɛn ye, hadamadenimaba dɔ, n’a bɛ ɲini ka jɔyɔrɔtigiya jogo ɲuman da,
Usumani Jara bangera zuwɛnkalo tile 29 san 1946 Bamakɔ, dugujukɔrɔfɛla ɲɛminɛni ɲɛmɔgɔ ye, a b’a ka hakɛw labolila san 2008 desanburukalo tile 31 san na, san cɛɲi ɲumanba kɔnɔ, an bɛ min ɲɛfɔ tan fɔlɔbaw la.
Ka sin faaba dugu cɛmancɛ fanfɛ, ntolan tun ye a farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɔnjɔn ye.
A kɛra Bamakɔ – Kura Olɛnpiki Sportsow la, walasa k’a o kɔ Bamakɔ – Kura olɛnpiki tɔn ( SEWOBE ) la, san 1962 – 1963.
A tora san tan kɔnɔ ni n’o ye tɔn jalatigi ye.
O waati kelen na, Usumani Jara ye ntola tan ni Bamakɔkura tɔnw, Askiya Mohamɛdi ka tɔnw ye.
ENA, Pari Dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkulu
Nɛyɛli ani Sangha Kulɔbu ka Tɔn nafolo bɛ min kɔnɔ.
San 1973 la, a b’a ka ntolatanna sɛgɛnnafiyɛnbɔ ta, k’a da a kan marako a ka waati administratifi baara tun t’a la a ka gɛlɛya kosɛbɛ k’a tɛgɛ kɛ.
K’a bɔ Moti la, a bilala Bamakɔ San 1976, wa o de ye waati min dilanna SEWOBE ɲɛmɔgɔw fɛ ka ko bɛɛ ɲɛbila walasa k’a ta ka taa disiriki Ligue la.
O de la, Usumani Jara ye sekeretɛri zenerali ɲɛmɔgɔya jɔyɔrɔ fa.
Ceba Kulibali, Adama Tarawore, Bakari Dosolo Tarawore, Jibirili Mayiga.
Zanwiyekalo tile 28 san 1978 kow ye Femmefiti ka toli an’a baaraw lakana.
Farikoloɲɛnajɛw baaradaba, min ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ Me Aliyumani Bɛye fɛ, ye Bamakɔ Ligi Jamana kolatigɛjɛkulu sigili sen kan, ulu kɔnɔ Usumani Jara bɛ Farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɔyɔrɔtigi ye ani Fasodenya Fémafuti jamana baarakɛjɛkulu, min kɔnɔ a bɛ kɛ a ye Farikoloɲɛnajɛ baarakɛjɛkulu perezidan ye.
San o san, ntolankuluw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ kologɛlɛyali kɛra Ligi ɲɛmɔgɔya la, ani Jamana biro perezidandankan, Kolonɛli Sɛki Jara bɛ min bolo,
Tuma min o laban cira baarada wɛrɛw la san 1986, Usumani Jara bɛ Mali ntolatan ɲɛminɛ ntola ɲɛ sigi sen kan san duuru kɔnɔ ( 1988 – 1992 ).
ininkali caman tun bɛ an kɛnɛ kan, ka ɲɛsin a ka saratiwaatiɲɔgɔnya koɲɛw ma.
nɔndɛmɛnɛya Nk’a ma sɔn nin dafiri la, walasa an k’i jilaja, n’a y’a sɔrɔ tuma bɛɛ, an nkalon to anw la, ka d’a kan ko bɛn kɛta dɔw dɔn.
Hali a ka bɔ Federason ka na, min ka fɔ anw kunnafoniw la tun b’a la ka kɛ wari lataa ɲɛ, o ma kɛ sababu ye ka fɔn dɔw kumaniya.
Ni Farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiriw ka baaraɲɔgɔnya ye, Usumani Jara sen bɛ ntolatanyɔrɔw la, ntolatanw baaraɲɔgɔnya taabolow ɲɛnabɔli cogoya kan Mali kɔnɔ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ yɛlɛma bakuruba fɔli la, hali n’a ma kɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye, n’a bɛ ɲini ka kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ yɛrɛyɛrɛ baarakɛnafolo la, n’a bɛ se ka kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ baarakɛnafolo la.
Ko ɲɔgɔnw tun bɛ Farikoloɲɛnajɛw baaradaba ni federason cɛ?
Jamana ntolatantɔnw ka jɔnjɔnw tun bɛ fa?
Jɛkulu ka kumakan tun b’a la ka ntolatannaw laɲini ni wari hakɛ caman ye wa?
« Farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiriso b’a bolo kan.
N’o ye ntolatan ɲɛmɔgɔyaso ka jɔyɔrɔtigiya ye, tɛna kɛ ka hierarchiya ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ jɛkulu fila ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A ko bɛɛ tun bɛ jɛɲɔgɔnna koɲuman, kumaɲɔgɔnya, laɲiniw tun bɛ kɛnɛ kan.
Jamana tun bɛ se ka dɔwɛrɛw ɲangi.
A baarakɛminɛn don, ɲɛmɔgɔw tun bɛ ka kɛ u ka kow ɲuman ye.
Kumasɛbɛn kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen tɛ ntolancilaw bolo, Federason donna degelikaramɔgɔw bolo, a ka fɛɛrɛw bɛɛ latigɛ kɔnɔ ».
A taali bɔ Jamana degelikaramɔgɔso la 1953, a bɛ san 1967 ka don Jamana foroba cakɛdaw ( ENA ) la.
A bɛ daminɛ ɔkutɔburukalo tile 15 san 1971, k’a kɛ dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ɲinininikɛla ye.
O la, a ka mara baaraw ni ɲɔgɔndan ɲuman bɛ daminɛ ni kalan fɔlɔ ye Faransi kɔnɔ san 1973.
Yanni a kɛlen ka nin sɛgɛsɛgɛli kama, a tun bɛ brigadi ɲɛmɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔ fa Faladi.
A seginnen na, a dira Moti marabolo jagowari ɲɛmɔgɔyaso la, k’a kɛ sababu ye ka ciw daminɛ.
Bamakɔ - Senou baarakɛjɛkulu, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw sɛgɛsɛgɛliw ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu, sɔrɔkow siratigɛw ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu, sariyaw ni baarabɛnkankow jɛkulu, fɛn kɛlenw ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu, sɔsɔliko biroɲɛmɔgɔ, sɔsɔliko biroɲɛmɔgɔ, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛdaw ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu ani ɲɛmɔgɔba, san 1991 san.
San 1991 marisikalo tɔgɔw kɔfɛ, Usumani Jara bilala durɔn, ni k’a ladilikɛla fɛɛrɛtigi, Sɔrɔ ani Jago minisiriso la, san kelen o kɔ, a bɛ jɔyɔrɔ kelenw fa minnu kɔnɔ, Sɔrɔ ani Plan minisiriso la.
San 1994, a bɛ kɛ Cakɛda baarakɛminɛnw ka Kumaso ni ɲɔgɔn nafolokow bolofara mɔgɔ ye.
O ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔfɛ, a bɛ segin ka na dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔyaso la, k’a dɛmɛni kama ɲɛ san 2008 laban na.
A ɲɛmajɔ jɛlen Usumani Jara ye kalo damadɔ kɛ, walasa k’a ka koɲɛnabɔ biro sigila, min ka baara kɛra degelikalan ani koɲɛnabɔliw kɛbagaw ye.
Federason perezidan kɔrɔ ye furu kɛ, ani den duuru hakɛ ye, k’a sɔrɔ denmisɛn caman bɛ a la.
Diɲɛnatigɛ la, a bɛ ntolatan, hadamadenw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Kumasurun na, an b’a hakilijigin kɛ ko Musafiti perezidan kɔrɔ, Usumani Jara, bɛ Mali ntolatan sankɔrɔtalenw kɔnɔ ni régionale kupu fɔlɔ ye, min dira Samatasɛgɛw fɛ 1989, Can denmisɛnw nɔkunbɛ finali, min dira Samatasɛgɛw fɛ, 1988, diɲɛ kupu tanna Arabiya jamana kan.
O. Oroze - Telefɔni ( 00223 ) 63 88 24 23.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu (SEYSIYA) y’a ka laadalatɔnsigi sabanan 43nan kɛ, zuwɛnkalo tile 29 san 2021, Bamakɔ.
Nin ɲɔgɔnyeba hakɛ tun ye k’a dɔn fɛn kan min kɛra bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali la sen kan ani ka kan ka bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali sen kan lakɔlɔsi.
Nin waatilabaara ye Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga, bisimilali kɛ SEYSIYA perezidan, Buweleli Sɛbihi, Alizeri lasigiden, Mali jamana kɔnɔ, Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, El-Gasimu WANE, min bɛ MINISIMA ( Misiyona multidimensionnelle ɲɛsigi, min bɛ tali kɛ Mali la ) ɲɛmɔgɔ ye ; fan bɛɛ fɛ sɔn bɛnkan (Governan-SEMA-Plateforme-Médiation ) la.
